    6               3                          2     
    7                                                
    8                                                        localparam int apb_read_access   = 0;
    9                                                        localparam int apb_write_access  = 1;
    10                                               
    11                                                       localparam int apb_ctrl_regs     = 0;
    12                                                       localparam int apb_status_regs   = 1;
    13                                                       localparam int apb_yield_regs    = 2;
    14                                                       localparam int apb_npk_regs      = 3;
    15                                                       localparam int apb_soil_regs     = 4;
    16                                                       localparam int apb_weather_regs  = 5;
    17                                                       localparam int apb_misc_regs     = 6;
    18                                                       localparam int apb_invalid_regs  = 7;
    19                                               
    20                                                       localparam int apb_strobe_none   = 0;
    21                                                       localparam int apb_strobe_full   = 1;
    22                                                       localparam int apb_strobe_low    = 2;
    23                                                       localparam int apb_strobe_high   = 3;
    24                                                       localparam int apb_strobe_other  = 4;
    25                                               
    26                                                       localparam int apb_ctrl_none     = 0;
    27                                                       localparam int apb_ctrl_write    = 1;
    28                                                       localparam int apb_ctrl_reset    = 2;
    29                                               
    30                                                       localparam int apb_status_none   = 0;
    31                                                       localparam int apb_status_busy   = 1;
    32                                                       localparam int apb_status_ready  = 2;
    33                                               
    34                                                       localparam int range_unknown     = 0;
    35                                                       localparam int range_negative    = 1;
    36                                                       localparam int range_zero        = 2;
    37                                                       localparam int range_low         = 3;
    38                                                       localparam int range_medium      = 4;
    39                                                       localparam int range_high        = 5;
    40                                                       localparam int range_extreme     = 6;
    41                                               
    42                                                       localparam int ph_unknown        = 0;
    43                                                       localparam int ph_acidic         = 1;
    44                                                       localparam int ph_neutral        = 2;
    45                                                       localparam int ph_alkaline       = 3;
    46                                               
    47                                                       localparam int flag_unknown      = 0;
    48                                                       localparam int flag_zero         = 1;
    49                                                       localparam int flag_one          = 2;
    50                                                       localparam int flag_other        = 3;
    51                                               
    52                                                       localparam int enum_unknown      = 0;
    53                                                       localparam int enum_zero         = 1;
    54                                                       localparam int enum_one          = 2;
    55                                                       localparam int enum_low          = 3;
    56                                                       localparam int enum_medium       = 4;
    57                                                       localparam int enum_high         = 5;
    58                                               
    59                                                       virtual cyp_apb_master_if master_if;
    60                                                       virtual cyp_apb_slave_if slave_if;
    61                                               
    62                                                       uvm_analysis_export #(cyp_seq_item) cov_export;
    63                                                       uvm_tlm_analysis_fifo #(cyp_seq_item) cov_cyp;
    64                                                       cyp_seq_item seq_item_cov;
    65                                                       cyp_apb_seq_item apb_seq_item_cov;
    66                                               
    67                                                       int apb_access_kind;
    68                                                       int apb_addr_kind;
    69                                                       int apb_strobe_kind;
    70                                                       int apb_ready_kind;
    71                                                       int apb_error_kind;
    72                                                       int apb_ctrl_kind;
    73                                                       int apb_status_kind;
    74                                               
    75                                                       int crop_rst_kind;
    76                                                       int crop_ready_kind;
    77                                                       int crop_npk_kind;
    78                                                       int crop_soil_ph_kind;
    79                                                       int crop_soil_moisture_kind;
    80                                                       int crop_temperature_kind;
    81                                                       int crop_rainfall_kind;
    82                                                       int crop_humidity_kind;
    83                                                       int crop_crop_type_kind;
    84                                                       int crop_irrigation_kind;
    85                                                       int crop_season_kind;
    86                                                       int crop_fertilizer_kind;
    87                                                       int crop_pesticide_kind;
    88                                                       int crop_yield_kind;
    89                                               
    90                                                       covergroup apb_cov_grp;
    91                                                           option.per_instance = 1;
    92                                               
    93                                                           cp_apb_access : coverpoint apb_access_kind {
    94                                                               bins read  = {apb_read_access};
    95                                                               bins write = {apb_write_access};
    96                                                           }
    97                                               
    98                                                           cp_apb_addr : coverpoint apb_addr_kind {
    99                                                               bins ctrl_regs    = {apb_ctrl_regs};
    100                                                              bins status_regs  = {apb_status_regs};
    101                                                              bins yield_regs   = {apb_yield_regs};
    102                                                              bins npk_regs     = {apb_npk_regs};
    103                                                              bins soil_regs    = {apb_soil_regs};
    104                                                              bins weather_regs = {apb_weather_regs};
    105                                                              bins misc_regs    = {apb_misc_regs};
    106                                                              ignore_bins invalid_regs = {apb_invalid_regs};
    107                                                          }
    108                                              
    109                                                          cp_apb_strobe : coverpoint apb_strobe_kind {
    110                                                              bins none = {apb_strobe_none};
    111                                                              bins full = {apb_strobe_full};
    112                                                              ignore_bins partial = {apb_strobe_low, apb_strobe_high, apb_strobe_other};
    113                                                          }
    114                                              
    115                                                          cp_apb_ready : coverpoint apb_ready_kind {
    116                                                              bins ready = {1};
    117                                                          }
    118                                              
    119                                                          cp_apb_error : coverpoint apb_error_kind {
    120                                                              bins no_error = {0};
    121                                                              ignore_bins error = {1};
    122                                                          }
    123                                              
    124                                                          cp_apb_ctrl : coverpoint apb_ctrl_kind {
    125                                                              bins none       = {apb_ctrl_none};
    126                                                              bins ctrl_reset = {apb_ctrl_reset};
    127                                                              ignore_bins ctrl_write = {apb_ctrl_write};
    128                                                          }
    129                                              
    130                                                          cp_apb_status : coverpoint apb_status_kind {
    131                                                              bins none  = {apb_status_none};
    132                                                              bins busy  = {apb_status_busy};
    133                                                              bins ready = {apb_status_ready};
    134                                                          }
    135                                              
    136                                                          cr_apb_access_addr : cross cp_apb_access, cp_apb_addr {
    137                                                              bins ctrl_write    = binsof(cp_apb_access.write) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.ctrl_regs);
    138                                                              bins status_read   = binsof(cp_apb_access.read)  && binsof(cp_apb_addr.status_regs);
    139                                                              bins yield_read    = binsof(cp_apb_access.read)  && binsof(cp_apb_addr.yield_regs);
    140                                                              bins npk_write     = binsof(cp_apb_access.write) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.npk_regs);
    141                                                              bins soil_write    = binsof(cp_apb_access.write) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.soil_regs);
    142                                                              bins weather_write = binsof(cp_apb_access.write) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.weather_regs);
    143                                                              bins misc_write    = binsof(cp_apb_access.write) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.misc_regs);
    144                                                          }
    145                                              
    146                                                          cr_apb_error_access : cross cp_apb_error, cp_apb_access {
    147                                                              bins clean_read  = binsof(cp_apb_error.no_error) && binsof(cp_apb_access.read);
    148                                                              bins clean_write = binsof(cp_apb_error.no_error) && binsof(cp_apb_access.write);
    149                                                          }
    150                                              
    151                                                          cr_apb_strobe_addr : cross cp_apb_strobe, cp_apb_addr {
    152                                                              bins ctrl_full    = binsof(cp_apb_strobe.full) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.ctrl_regs);
    153                                                              bins status_none  = binsof(cp_apb_strobe.none) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.status_regs);
    154                                                              bins yield_none   = binsof(cp_apb_strobe.none) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.yield_regs);
    155                                                              bins npk_full     = binsof(cp_apb_strobe.full) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.npk_regs);
    156                                                              bins soil_full    = binsof(cp_apb_strobe.full) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.soil_regs);
    157                                                              bins weather_full = binsof(cp_apb_strobe.full) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.weather_regs);
    158                                                              bins misc_full    = binsof(cp_apb_strobe.full) && binsof(cp_apb_addr.misc_regs);
    159                                                          }
    160                                                      endgroup : apb_cov_grp
    161                                              
    162                                                      covergroup cyp_cov_grp;
    163                                                          option.per_instance = 1;
    164                                              
    165                                                          cp_crop_rst : coverpoint crop_rst_kind {
    166                                                              bins rst_off = {0};
    167                                                              bins rst_on  = {1};
    168                                                          }
    169                                              
    170                                                          cp_crop_ready : coverpoint crop_ready_kind {
    171                                                              bins ready = {1};
    172                                                          }
    173                                              
    174                                                          cp_crop_npk : coverpoint crop_npk_kind {
    175                                                              bins zero   = {range_zero};
    176                                                              bins normal = {range_low, range_medium};
    177                                                              bins rich   = {range_high, range_extreme};
    178                                                              ignore_bins unused = {range_unknown, range_negative};
    179                                                          }
    180                                              
    181                                                          cp_crop_soil_ph : coverpoint crop_soil_ph_kind {
    182                                                              bins acidic   = {ph_acidic};
    183                                                              bins neutral  = {ph_neutral};
    184                                                              bins alkaline = {ph_alkaline};
    185                                                          }
    186                                              
    187                                                          cp_crop_soil_moisture : coverpoint crop_soil_moisture_kind {
    188                                                              bins zero = {range_zero};
    189                                                              bins dry  = {range_low};
    190                                                              bins wet  = {range_medium, range_high, range_extreme};
    191                                                              ignore_bins unused = {range_unknown, range_negative};
    192                                                          }
    193                                              
    194                                                          cp_crop_temperature : coverpoint crop_temperature_kind {
    195                                                              bins zero = {range_zero};
    196                                                              bins mild = {range_low, range_medium};
    197                                                              bins hot  = {range_high, range_extreme};
    198                                                              ignore_bins unused = {range_unknown, range_negative};
    199                                                          }
    200                                              
    201                                                          cp_crop_rainfall : coverpoint crop_rainfall_kind {
    202                                                              bins zero   = {range_zero};
    203                                                              bins active = {range_low, range_medium, range_high, range_extreme};
    204                                                              ignore_bins unused = {range_unknown, range_negative};
    205                                                          }
    206                                              
    207                                                          cp_crop_humidity : coverpoint crop_humidity_kind {
    208                                                              bins zero   = {range_zero};
    209                                                              bins normal = {range_low, range_medium};
    210                                                              bins humid  = {range_high, range_extreme};
    211                                                              ignore_bins unused = {range_unknown, range_negative};
    212                                                          }
    213                                              
    214                                                          cp_crop_type : coverpoint crop_crop_type_kind {
    215                                                              bins unknown = {enum_unknown};
    216                                                              bins base    = {enum_zero, enum_one};
    217                                                              bins active  = {enum_low, enum_medium, enum_high};
    218                                                          }
    219                                              
    220                                                          cp_crop_irrigation : coverpoint crop_irrigation_kind {
    221                                                              bins unknown = {enum_unknown};
    222                                                              bins base    = {enum_zero, enum_one};
    223                                                              bins active  = {enum_low, enum_medium, enum_high};
    224                                                          }
    225                                              
    226                                                          cp_crop_season : coverpoint crop_season_kind {
    227                                                              bins unknown = {enum_unknown};
    228                                                              bins base    = {enum_zero, enum_one};
    229                                                              bins active  = {enum_low, enum_medium, enum_high};
    230                                                          }
    231                                              
    232                                                          cp_crop_fertilizer : coverpoint crop_fertilizer_kind {
    233                                                              bins zero   = {flag_zero};
    234                                                              bins active = {flag_one, flag_other};
    235                                                              ignore_bins unknown = {flag_unknown};
    236                                                          }
    237                                              
    238                                                          cp_crop_pesticide : coverpoint crop_pesticide_kind {
    239                                                              bins unknown = {flag_unknown};
    240                                                              bins zero    = {flag_zero};
    241                                                              bins active  = {flag_one, flag_other};
    242                                                          }
    243                                              
    244                                                          cp_crop_yield : coverpoint crop_yield_kind {
    245                                                              bins med  = {range_medium};
    246                                                              bins high = {range_high, range_extreme};
    247                                                              ignore_bins unused = {range_unknown, range_negative, range_zero, range_low};
    248                                                          }
    249                                              
    250                                                          cr_npk_yield : cross cp_crop_npk, cp_crop_yield {
    251                                                              bins zero_to_med     = binsof(cp_crop_npk.zero)   && binsof(cp_crop_yield.med);
    252                                                              bins active_to_high  = binsof(cp_crop_npk.normal) && binsof(cp_crop_yield.high);
    253                                                              bins rich_to_high    = binsof(cp_crop_npk.rich)   && binsof(cp_crop_yield.high);
    254                                                          }
    255                                              
    256                                                          cr_soil_moisture_yield : cross cp_crop_soil_moisture, cp_crop_yield {
    257                                                              bins zero_to_med    = binsof(cp_crop_soil_moisture.zero) && binsof(cp_crop_yield.med);
    258                                                              bins dry_to_high    = binsof(cp_crop_soil_moisture.dry)  && binsof(cp_crop_yield.high);
    259                                                              bins wet_to_high    = binsof(cp_crop_soil_moisture.wet)  && binsof(cp_crop_yield.high);
    260                                                          }
    261                                              
    262                                                          cr_crop_type_yield : cross cp_crop_type, cp_crop_yield {
    263                                                              bins base_to_med    = binsof(cp_crop_type.base)    && binsof(cp_crop_yield.med);
    264                                                              bins active_to_high = binsof(cp_crop_type.active)  && binsof(cp_crop_yield.high);
    265                                                              bins unknown_seen   = binsof(cp_crop_type.unknown) && binsof(cp_crop_yield.high);
    266                                                          }
    267                                                      endgroup : cyp_cov_grp
    268                                              
    269                                                      function new (string name = "cyp_coverage", uvm_component parent);
    270             1                          1                 super.new(name, parent);
    271             1                          1                 apb_cov_grp = new();
    272             1                          1                 cyp_cov_grp = new();
    273                                                      endfunction : new
    274                                              
    275                                                      function void build_phase(uvm_phase phase);
    276             1                          1                 super.build_phase(phase);
    277             1                          1                 cov_export = new("cov_export", this);
    278             1                          1                 cov_cyp = new("cov_cyp", this);
    279                                              
    280                                                          if(!uvm_config_db #(virtual cyp_apb_master_if)::get(this,"","master_if",master_if))
    281             1                    ***0***                     `uvm_warning("build_phase","Unable to get master_if from the database")
    282                                              
    283                                                          if(!uvm_config_db #(virtual cyp_apb_slave_if)::get(this,"","slave_if",slave_if))
    284             1                    ***0***                     `uvm_warning("build_phase","Unable to get slave_if from the database")
    285                                                      endfunction : build_phase
    286                                              
    287                                                      function void connect_phase(uvm_phase phase);
    288             1                          1                 super.connect_phase(phase);
    289             1                          1                 cov_export.connect(cov_cyp.analysis_export);
    290                                                      endfunction : connect_phase
    291                                              
    292                                                      task run_phase(uvm_phase phase);
    293             1                          1                 super.run_phase(phase);
    294                                                          fork
    295             1                          1                     forever begin
    296             1                      10002                         cov_cyp.get(seq_item_cov);
    297             1                      10001                         sample_crop_item(seq_item_cov);
    298                                                              end
    299                                              
    300                                                              if (slave_if != null) begin
    301             1                          1                         forever begin
    302             1                    1680004                             @(posedge slave_if.pclk);
    303                                                                      if (slave_if.psel && slave_if.penable && slave_if.pready) begin
    304             1                     839999                                 apb_seq_item_cov = cyp_apb_seq_item::type_id::create("apb_seq_item_cov");
    305                                              
    306             1                     839999                                 apb_seq_item_cov.write  = slave_if.pwrite;
    307             1                     839999                                 apb_seq_item_cov.addr   = slave_if.paddr;
    308             1                     839999                                 apb_seq_item_cov.wdata  = slave_if.pwdata;
    309             1                     839999                                 apb_seq_item_cov.strb   = slave_if.pstrb;
    310             1                     839999                                 apb_seq_item_cov.prot   = slave_if.pprot;
    311             1                     839999                                 apb_seq_item_cov.rdata  = slave_if.prdata;
    312             1                     839999                                 apb_seq_item_cov.ready  = slave_if.pready;
    313             1                     839999                                 apb_seq_item_cov.slverr = slave_if.pslverr;
    314                                              
    315             1                     839999                                 sample_apb_item(apb_seq_item_cov);
    316                                                                      end
    317                                                                  end
    318                                                              end
    319                                                              else if (master_if != null) begin
    320             1                    ***0***                         forever begin
    321             1                    ***0***                             @(posedge master_if.pclk);
    322                                                                      if (master_if.transfer && master_if.pready) begin
    323             1                    ***0***                                 apb_seq_item_cov = cyp_apb_seq_item::type_id::create("apb_seq_item_cov");
    324                                              
    325             1                    ***0***                                 apb_seq_item_cov.write  = master_if.swrite;
    326             1                    ***0***                                 apb_seq_item_cov.addr   = master_if.saddr;
    327             1                    ***0***                                 apb_seq_item_cov.wdata  = master_if.swdata;
    328             1                    ***0***                                 apb_seq_item_cov.strb   = master_if.sstrb;
    329             1                    ***0***                                 apb_seq_item_cov.prot   = master_if.sprot;
    330             1                    ***0***                                 apb_seq_item_cov.rdata  = master_if.prdata;
    331             1                    ***0***                                 apb_seq_item_cov.ready  = master_if.pready;
    332             1                    ***0***                                 apb_seq_item_cov.slverr = master_if.pslverr;
    333                                              
    334             1                    ***0***                                 sample_apb_item(apb_seq_item_cov);
    335                                                                      end
    336                                                                  end
    337                                                              end
    338                                                          join
    339                                                      endtask : run_phase
    340                                              
    341                                                      function void sample_apb_item(cyp_apb_seq_item item);
    342             1                     839999                 apb_access_kind = item.write ? apb_write_access : apb_read_access;
    343             1                     839999                 apb_addr_kind   = get_apb_addr_kind(item.addr);
    344             1                     839999                 apb_strobe_kind = get_apb_strobe_kind(item.strb);
    345             1                     839999                 apb_ready_kind  = item.ready;
    346             1                     839999                 apb_error_kind  = item.slverr;
    347             1                     839999                 apb_ctrl_kind   = get_apb_ctrl_kind(item);
    348             1                     839999                 apb_status_kind = get_apb_status_kind(item);
    349             1                     839999                 apb_cov_grp.sample();
    350                                                      endfunction : sample_apb_item
    351                                              
    352                                                      function void sample_crop_item(cyp_seq_item item);
    353             1                      10001                 crop_rst_kind           = item.rst;
    354             1                      10001                 crop_ready_kind         = item.ready;
    355             1                      10001                 crop_npk_kind           = get_average_bucket(item.N, item.P, item.K, 40.0, 80.0, 160.0);
    356             1                      10001                 crop_soil_ph_kind       = get_ph_bucket(item.soil_ph);
    357             1                      10001                 crop_soil_moisture_kind = get_range_bucket(item.soil_moisture, 20.0, 40.0, 60.0);
    358             1                      10001                 crop_temperature_kind   = get_range_bucket(item.temperature, 15.0, 30.0, 40.0);
    359             1                      10001                 crop_rainfall_kind      = get_range_bucket(item.rainfall, 100.0, 500.0, 1000.0);
    360             1                      10001                 crop_humidity_kind      = get_range_bucket(item.humidity, 30.0, 70.0, 90.0);
    361             1                      10001                 crop_crop_type_kind     = get_enum_bucket(item.crop_type, 3, 7);
    362             1                      10001                 crop_irrigation_kind    = get_enum_bucket(item.irrigation_type, 2, 5);
    363             1                      10001                 crop_season_kind        = get_enum_bucket(item.season, 2, 4);
    364             1                      10001                 crop_fertilizer_kind    = get_flag_bucket(item.fertilizer_used);
    365             1                      10001                 crop_pesticide_kind     = get_flag_bucket(item.pesticide_used);
    366             1                      10001                 crop_yield_kind         = get_range_bucket(item.yield_int, 1.0, 5.0, 10.0);
    367             1                      10001                 cyp_cov_grp.sample();
    368                                                      endfunction : sample_crop_item
    369                                              
    370                                                      function int get_apb_addr_kind(logic [`APB_ADDR_WIDTH-1:0] addr);
    371                                                          case (addr)
    372             1                      20000                     `CTRL_ADDR                    : return apb_ctrl_regs;
    373             1                      20000                     `STATUS_ADDR                  : return apb_status_regs;
    374             1                      40000                     `YIELD_L_ADDR, `YIELD_H_ADDR  : return apb_yield_regs;
    375                                              
    376                                                              `N_L_ADDR, `N_H_ADDR,
    377                                                              `P_L_ADDR, `P_H_ADDR,
    378             1                     119999                     `K_L_ADDR, `K_H_ADDR          : return apb_npk_regs;
    379                                              
    380                                                              `SOIL_PH_L_ADDR, `SOIL_PH_H_ADDR,
    381                                                              `SOIL_MOISTURE_L_ADDR, `SOIL_MOISTURE_H_ADDR,
    382                                                              `ORGANIC_CARBON_L_ADDR, `ORGANIC_CARBON_H_ADDR,
    383             1                     160000                     `SOIL_TYPE_L_ADDR, `SOIL_TYPE_H_ADDR : return apb_soil_regs;
    384                                              
    385                                                              `TEMPERATURE_L_ADDR, `TEMPERATURE_H_ADDR,
    386                                                              `RAINFALL_L_ADDR, `RAINFALL_H_ADDR,
    387                                                              `SUNLIGHT_HOURS_L_ADDR, `SUNLIGHT_HOURS_H_ADDR,
    388                                                              `WIND_SPEED_L_ADDR, `WIND_SPEED_H_ADDR,
    389             1                     200000                     `HUMIDITY_L_ADDR, `HUMIDITY_H_ADDR : return apb_weather_regs;
    390                                              
    391                                                              `CROP_TYPE_L_ADDR, `CROP_TYPE_H_ADDR,
    392                                                              `FERTILIZER_USED_L_ADDR, `FERTILIZER_USED_H_ADDR,
    393                                                              `ALTITUDE_L_ADDR, `ALTITUDE_H_ADDR,
    394                                                              `REGION_L_ADDR, `REGION_H_ADDR,
    395                                                              `IRRIGATION_TYPE_L_ADDR, `IRRIGATION_TYPE_H_ADDR,
    396                                                              `SEASON_L_ADDR, `SEASON_H_ADDR,
    397             1                     280000                     `PESTICIDE_USED_L_ADDR, `PESTICIDE_USED_H_ADDR : return apb_misc_regs;
    398                                              
    399             1                    ***0***                     default : return apb_invalid_regs;
    400                                                          endcase
    401                                                      endfunction : get_apb_addr_kind
    402                                              
    403                                                      function int get_apb_strobe_kind(logic [`APB_STRB_WIDTH-1:0] strb);
    404                                                          case (strb)
    405             1                      60000                     4'b0000 : return apb_strobe_none;
    406             1                     779999                     4'b1111 : return apb_strobe_full;
    407             1                    ***0***                     4'b0011 : return apb_strobe_low;
    408             1                    ***0***                     4'b1100 : return apb_strobe_high;
    409             1                    ***0***                     default : return apb_strobe_other;
    410                                                          endcase

    160                                                  function void check_results(logic [63:0] dut_yield_int, int cycle);
    161                                              
    162                                                      if (cycle >= predicted_yield_mem.size() || cycle >= actual_yield_mem.size())
    163             1                    ***0***                 return;
    164                                              
    165             1                      10000             yield_int = dut_yield_int;
    166                                              
    167             1                      10000             yield_real = $bitstoreal(yield_int);
    168             1                      10000             pred_real  = $bitstoreal(predicted_yield_mem[cycle]);
    169             1                      10000             act_real   = $bitstoreal(actual_yield_mem[cycle]);
    170                                              
    171             1                      10000             tolerance_p = 0.01 * (pred_real >= 0 ? pred_real : -pred_real);
    172             1                      10000             tolerance_a = 0.2 * (act_real >= 0 ? act_real : -act_real);
    173                                              
    174             1                      10000             diff_pred = yield_real - pred_real;
    175             1                       4737             if (diff_pred < 0.0) diff_pred = -diff_pred;
    176             1                      10000             error_pred_pct = 100.0 * diff_pred / (pred_real != 0.0 ? pred_real : 1.0);
    177                                              
    178             1                      10000             diff_act = yield_real - act_real;
    179             1                       4946             if (diff_act < 0.0) diff_act = -diff_act;
    180             1                      10000             error_act_pct = 100.0 * diff_act / (act_real != 0.0 ? act_real : 1.0);
    181                                              
    182                                                      if (diff_pred > tolerance_p) begin
    183             1                    ***0***                 error_count_predicted++;
    184             1                    ***0***                 `uvm_error("MISMATCH_PRED",
    185                                                              $sformatf("Cycle %0d: DUT Yield=%.6f Expected Predicted=%.6f (error = %.2f%%)",
    186                                                                        cycle, yield_real, pred_real, error_pred_pct));
    187                                                      end
    188                                                      else begin
    189             1                      10000                 correct_count_predicted++;
    190             1                    ***0***                 `uvm_info("Correct", 
    191                                                        $sformatf("Cycle %0d: DUT Yield=%.6f Expected Predicted=%.6f (error = %.2f%%)",
    192                                                                  cycle, yield_real, pred_real, error_pred_pct),
    193                                                        UVM_HIGH)
    194                                                      end
    195                                              
    196                                                      if (diff_act > tolerance_a) begin
    197             1                        750                 error_count_actual++;
    198                                                      end
    199                                                      else begin
    200             1                       9250                 correct_count_actual++;

    52              1                          1                 cyp_reset_seq.start(env.master_agent.cyp_seqr);
